The good news is that the food here is absolutely delicious, we had the pizza panini and create your own salad, and both were perfectly satisfying.  The staff were helpful and the place overall was clean and decorated tastefully.

However I can‚Äôt in good conscience give this place a full 5 stars because they were advertising about 5 specials and were out of ingredients for at least two of them (my first and second choices).  One was the jackfruit salad or panini, can‚Äôt remember exactly, and I can‚Äôt remember the other.  Apparently there was a lunch rush that used up the main ingredients.  The problem was that even though they were out of two specials they left the signs up for them.  Then, at least two times the employees offered to help me with ordering, but neither time did they inform me they were out of the specials.  I only found out when I actually tried to order one, and then after being disappointed, tried to order the second, which of course was out too.  This is not a problem necessarily with food stocking, but more a problem of good employee training.  Sometimes I go into a restaurant after looking at the specials I see advertised, and when they‚Äôre out, it feels a little like a bait and switch, even if it‚Äôs unintentional.<//Text>

First time going to this place.  We tried a few times but it wasn't open yet at the time.  We had breakfast and I chose the sweet panini sandwich and the salad.  The drinks were delicious. <rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I've been coming here for years and honestly I no longer trust anyone else except Katie with my hair.

They have really stepped up to the plate during COVID. Everyone wears a mask the entire time. I didn't see any of that "let me rest my mask on my chin, or let my nose peek out" silliness from any of the staff or the guests. You check in outside and they read your temperature. Once you're inside, there's lots of room so you're always distanced from other guests. Everything is kept super clean. They also have an outdoor patio for even more room. The entire experience feels very safe for both you and the staff. It does not feel exploitative in any way. This has been really important to me as I evaluate what businesses to visit during this time - I never want to put anyone working at risk.

Yes, it is going to be more expensive than other salons, but it's a high end salon with quality to match. In this case you do get what you pay for and it's very worth it. Everyone there works extremely hard and is very skilled from what I've seen.

I highly recommend this place. Thank you Salon 1322 for giving me a bright spot to feel pampered (in a safe way) during this crazy time!< /Text>

< review>
I had been putting off getting my hair done for awhile because I was nervous about COVID. But I wanted to get a cut and style before my engagement photos, and decided to try Salon 1322 for the first time. I felt completely at ease from the moment I arrived at the salon. The check-in process was very safe, and they are adamant about limiting the amount of people inside the salon. After checking in on the iPad outside of the salon, Deb came to take my temperature and bring me to my chair. Staff members wore their masks at all times, and I never came in close contact with anyone besides my stylist. The salon was very clean and I was seated far away from any other customers. I washed my hair before my appointment, something they recommend to limit your time in the salon (this is totally optional though, if you like getting your hair washed at a salon you still can). I got a beautiful cut and curl, and felt totally safe the entire time. I really appreciate businesses that put their customers' health first. Salon 1322 will definitely be my new regular hair place!< /review>

In addition, Salon 1322 has also created a great outdoor salon area that also adheres to all COVID protocols, for those times when indoor services are not allowed.  I feel extremely safe at Salon 1322 and would not hesitate to book appointments there during these unsettling times.<//review>

Update: After months of shopping here I've been really disappointed by the fact they advertise meat prices but never seem to have any.  The staff isn't very helpful either and I've decided not to shop here anymore. I would recommend the Ralphs on 4th.

I found some things to be a good price here and others to be over priced. The produce did seem fresh and looked great. Meat selection had some good variety for beef with some really large cuts that would be good for a meat smoker but expensive. I'm probably just going to come here when things are on sale for what I need. As far as the staff goes, I kind of found them to be unprofessional. Unlike most stores in South Long Beach, this is a regular - sized Smart and Final Extra. It has everything any other SFE would have. <user_id>112593555821099772100<//user_id><user_name>DAVA MUNYON<//user_name><date>1621014338882<//date>< rate>
5<//rate>
<Review>OMG this was one of my best experiences with a hairstylist! I had the pleasure of working with Zach who took me on my journey from long hair to short hair. He was very helpful in helping me figure out what I want, explaining how to take care of my curly/wavy hair, and making me feel very comfortable with him. We laughed SO MUCH! I even told him about my previous experience with a hair dresser who had burned my scalp a little because they put the hairdryer on for too long, and he immediately told me that I should always let my hairdresser know if it's getting too hot.
